The family room I booked is actually a combination of a king-size bed room and a standard room, with a door connecting the two rooms. There are a lot of koi in the hotel, and there is fish food at the front desk, which the children like very much. There are many breakfast options, starting at 6:30, which is very convenient for going out in the morning.

The service is in place, providing a special butler service, and giving targeted suggestions for surrounding tours, which is very detailed!
The New Year spent here is very a**ospheric, with a festive a**osphere, and there is a lion dance on the morning of the first day of the new year, which is a surprise!
The location is suitable, not far from the surrounding scenic spots and streets, and it is convenient for life and play.
I stayed for four nights and was generally happy and satisfied.
